         <section class="body">
          <img alt="Lemon Curd Cupcakes" src="http://communitytable.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/5956399147_2e374d4b86_b.jpg" style="display:none"/>
          <div class="figure_block feature" data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="featured-image" data-parade-location-types="media" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="media" data-parade-views="false">
           <figure>
            <img alt="peach-mojito-cupcakes-picture" class="addthis_shareable" data-parade-image="" data-parade-image-placeholding="" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/peach-mojito-cupcakes-picture.jpg"/>
           </figure>
           <div class="parade-gallery-bug-container" data-parade-launch-gallery="395447">
            <div class="parade-gallery-bug" data-parade-clicks="true" data-parade-launch-gallery="395447" data-parade-location-ids="gallery-launch-bug" data-parade-location-types="promoarea" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="promoarea" data-parade-views="false">
             <div class="parade-gallery-bug-text" data-parade-launch-gallery="395447">
              Launch Gallery
             </div>
             <div class="parade-gallery-bug-meta" data-parade-launch-gallery="395447">
              20 Photos
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <span data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="article" data-parade-location-types="promoarea" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="promoarea" data-parade-views="false">
           <p class="first">
            I may be a certified chocoholic, but I
            <em>
             do
            </em>
            recognize the existence of fruit lovers so this one is for
            <strong>
             you
            </strong>
            ! Dont worry, I wouldnt
            <em>
             dare
            </em>
            pass up a delicious peach mojito cupcake or a coconut cupcake  yum! In fact, these 20 cupcakes for fruit lovers are over the top delicious and certainly give reason to pass on plain box cake mixes. The summer is the perfect season for embracing fruits like blackberries, strawberries, peaches, and pineapples. Whether you head to a farm and pick your own or even grow them in your backyard, youll have a sweet reason to pull the mixer out. From summer birthdays to patriotic holidays, whip up a dozen of any of these fruity cupcakes and your friends and family will love you, even if theyrechocolate lovers! Trust me.
           </p>
           <div class="figure_block size-100 alignnone">
            <figure>
             <a href="http://communitytable.parade.com/395568/20-fruit-cupcake-recipes/">
              <img alt="" class="addthis_shareable at_include" data-parade-image="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/20-fruit-cupcake-recipes.jpg" data-parade-image-inlining="" data-parade-image-placeholding="true" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/themes/wp-theme/img/misc/tiny.gif"/>
             </a>
            </figure>
           </div>
          </span>
